  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'CarRental' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'CarRental' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search vehicles, book rentals, manage reservations, view rental history, and select insurance options. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'CarRental' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'CarRental' web application will consist of the following nine pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Car Rental Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured vehicles, current promotions, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-vehicles** - Type: Div - Display of featured vehicle recommendations.   - **ID: search-vehicles-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to vehicle search page.   - **ID: my-reservations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to reservations page.   - **ID: promotions-section** - Type: Div - Display of current promotions and offers.  ### 2. Vehicle Search Page - **Page Title**: Search Vehicles - **Overview**: A page displaying all available vehicles with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.   - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by pickup location.   - **ID: vehicle-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by vehicle type (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury).   - **ID: date-range-input** - Type: Input - Field to select rental date range.   - **ID: vehicles-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying vehicle cards with image, model, price per day.   - **ID: view-details-button-{vehicle_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view vehicle details (each vehicle card has this).  ### 3. Vehicle Details Page - **Page Title**: Vehicle Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific vehicle. - **Elements**:   - **ID: vehicle-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the vehicle details page.   - **ID: vehicle-name** - Type: H1 - Display vehicle name and model.   - **ID: vehicle-specs** - Type: Div - Display vehicle specifications (engine, seats, transmission).   - **ID: daily-rate** - Type: Div - Display daily rental rate.   - **ID: book-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to book this vehicle.   - **ID: vehicle-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.  ### 4. Booking Page - **Page Title**: Book Your Rental - **Overview**: A page for users to complete rental booking with dates and location selection. - **Elements**:   - **ID: booking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the booking page.   - **ID: pickup-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select pickup location.   - **ID: dropoff-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select dropoff location.   - **ID: pickup-date** - Type: Input - Field to select pickup date.   - **ID: dropoff-date** - Type: Input - Field to select dropoff date.   - **ID: calculate-price-button** - Type: Button - Button to calculate total rental price.   - **ID: total-price** - Type: Div - Display calculated total price.   - **ID: proceed-to-insurance-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to insurance options.  ### 5. Insurance Options Page - **Page Title**: Select Insurance Coverage - **Overview**: A page for users to select insurance coverage for their rental. - **Elements**:   - **ID: insurance-page** - Type: Div - Container for the insurance page.   - **ID: insurance-options** - Type: Div - Display of available insurance plans.   - **ID: select-insurance-{insurance_id}** - Type: Radio - Radio button to select insurance plan (each plan has this).   - **ID: insurance-description** - Type: Div - Display description of selected insurance plan.   - **ID: insurance-price** - Type: Div - Display insurance price.   - **ID: confirm-booking-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm booking with insurance selection.  ### 6. Rental History Page - **Page Title**: Rental History - **Overview**: A page displaying all previous rentals with details and status information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: history-page** - Type: Div - Container for the rental history page.   - **ID: rentals-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying rentals with ID, vehicle, dates, location, and status.   - **ID: view-rental-details-{rental_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view rental details (each rental has this).   - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Active, Completed, Cancelled).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Reservation Management Page - **Page Title**: My Reservations - **Overview**: A page displaying current and upcoming reservations with management options. - **Elements**:   - **ID: reservations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reservations page.   - **ID: reservations-list** - Type: Div - List of all reservations with vehicle, dates, and status.   - **ID: modify-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to modify reservation (each reservation has this).   - **ID: cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel reservation (each reservation has this).   - **ID: sort-by-date-button** - Type: Button - Button to sort reservations by date.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Special Requests Page - **Page Title**: Special Requests - **Overview**: A page for users to add special requests to their rental booking. - **Elements**:   - **ID: requests-page** - Type: Div - Container for the special requests page.   - **ID: select-reservation** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select reservation to add requests to.   - **ID: driver-assistance-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for driver assistance request.   - **ID: gps-option-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for GPS option.   - **ID: child-seat-quantity** - Type: Input - Field to specify number of child seats needed.   - **ID: special-notes** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter special notes and requests.   - **ID: submit-requests-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit special requests.  ### 9. Locations Page - **Page Title**: Pickup and Dropoff Locations - **Overview**: A page displaying all available rental pickup and dropoff locations with details. - **Elements**:   - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.   - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all rental locations with address and hours.   - **ID: location-detail-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view location details (each location has this).   - **ID: hours-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by operating hours (24/7, Business Hours, Weekend).   - **ID: search-location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city or name.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'CarRental' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Vehicles Data - **File Name**: `vehicles.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available   2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available   3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available   ```  ### 2. Customers Data - **File Name**: `customers.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15   2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20   ```  ### 3. Locations Data - **File Name**: `locations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12   2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8   ```  ### 4. Rentals Data - **File Name**: `rentals.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed   2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active   ```  ### 5. Insurance Data - **File Name**: `insurance.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000   2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500   3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0   ```  ### 6. Reservations Data - **File Name**: `reservations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested   2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed   ```

Special Requests Page\n- Filename: templates/special_requests.html\n- Page Title: Special Requests\n- Element IDs:\n  - requests-page (Div): Root container\n  - select-reservation (Dropdown): Select reservation to add requests\n  - driver-assistance-checkbox (Checkbox): Driver assistance option\n  - gps-option-checkbox (Checkbox): GPS option\n  - child-seat-quantity (Input): Number of child seats\n  - special-notes (Textarea): Additional notes\n  - submit-requests-button (Button): Submit special requests\n- Navigation:\n  - submit-requests-button: url_for('special_requests')\n- Context Variables:\n  - reservations: list of dict with reservations\n\n\n### 9. Locations Page\n- Filename: templates/locations.html\n- Page Title: Pickup and Dropoff Locations\n- Element IDs:\n  - locations-page (Div): Root container\n  - locations-list (Div): List of locations\n  - location-detail-button-{location_id} (Button): View location details (dynamic)\n  - hours-filter (Dropdown): Filter by hours\n  - search-location-input (Input): Search locations field\n  - back-to-dashboard (Button): Back to dashboard\n- Navigation:\n  - location-detail-button-{location_id}: url_for('locations_page', location_id=location_id)\n  - back-to-dashboard: url_for('dashboard')\n- Context Variables:\n  - locations: list of dict with location info\n  - hours_filter: str filter applied to hours\n  - search_query: str for location search\n\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas\n\n### 1. vehicles.txt\n- Stores vehicle details for rental\n- Format (pipe-delimited, no header):\n  vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status\n- Data Types:\n  - vehicle_id: int\n  - make: str\n  - model: str\n  - vehicle_type: str (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury)\n  - daily_rate: float\n  - seats: int\n  - transmission: str (e.g., Automatic, Manual)\n  - fuel_type: str (e.g., Petrol, Diesel)\n  - status: str (Available, Rented, Maintenance)\n- Examples:\n```\n1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available\n2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available\n3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available\n```\n\n### 2. customers.txt\n- Stores customer information\n- Format:\n  customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry\n- Data Types:\n  - customer_id: int\n  - name: str\n  - email: str\n  - phone: str\n  - driver_license: str\n  - license_expiry: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Examples:\n```\n1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15\n2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20\n```\n\n### 3. locations.txt\n- Stores rental locations details\n- Format:\n  location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles\n- Data Types:\n  - location_id: int\n  - city: str\n  - address: str\n  - phone: str\n  - hours: str (e.g., '24/7', '09:00-18:00')\n  - available_vehicles: int\n- Examples:\n```\n1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12\n2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8\n```\n\n### 4. rentals.txt\n- Stores rental transaction details\n- Format:\n  rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status\n- Data Types:\n  - rental_id: int\n  - vehicle_id: int\n  - customer_id: int\n  - pickup_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - dropoff_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - pickup_location: str\n  - dropoff_location: str\n  - total_price: float\n  - status: str (Completed, Active, Cancelled)\n- Examples:\n```\n1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed\n2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active\n```\n\n### 5. insurance.txt\n- Stores insurance plan options\n- Format:\n  insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible\n- Data Types:\n  - insurance_id: int\n  - plan_name: str\n  - description: str\n  - daily_cost: float\n  - coverage_limit: str (e.g., 50000, 250000, 'Unlimited')\n  - deductible: int\n- Examples:\n```\n1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000\n2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500\n3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0\n```\n\n### 6. reservations.txt\n- Stores reservation details linked to rentals\n- Format:\n  reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests\n- Data Types:\n  - reservation_id: int\n  - rental_id: int\n  - vehicle_id: int\n  - customer_id: int\n  - status: str (Confirmed, Active, Cancelled)\n  - insurance_id: int\n  - special_requests: str\n- Examples:\n```\n1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested\n2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed\n```\n\n---\n\nThis design specification fully encapsulates the backend route requirements, frontend HTML template structures, and data file schemas for CarRental app development without cross-dependent code or assumptions beyond given requirements."})

Language The required development language for the 'CarRental' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'CarRental' web application will consist of the following nine pages:  ### 1. Vehicle Search Page - **Page Title**: Search Vehicles - **Overview**: A page displaying all available vehicles with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.   - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by pickup location.   - **ID: vehicle-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by vehicle type (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury).   - **ID: date-range-input** - Type: Input - Field to select rental date range.   - **ID: vehicles-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying vehicle cards with image, model, price per day.   - **ID: view-details-button-{vehicle_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view vehicle details (each vehicle card has this).  ### 3. Vehicle Details Page - **Page Title**: Vehicle Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific vehicle. - **Elements**:   - **ID: vehicle-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the vehicle details page.   - **ID: vehicle-name** - Type: H1 - Display vehicle name and model.   - **ID: vehicle-specs** - Type: Div - Display vehicle specifications (engine, seats, transmission).   - **ID: daily-rate** - Type: Div - Display daily rental rate.   - **ID: book-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to book this vehicle.   - **ID: vehicle-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.  ### 4. Booking Page - **Page Title**: Book Your Rental - **Overview**: A page for users to complete rental booking with dates and location selection. - **Elements**:   - **ID: booking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the booking page.   - **ID: pickup-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select pickup location.   - **ID: dropoff-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select dropoff location.   - **ID: pickup-date** - Type: Input - Field to select pickup date.   - **ID: dropoff-date** - Type: Input - Field to select dropoff date.   - **ID: calculate-price-button** - Type: Button - Button to calculate total rental price.   - **ID: total-price** - Type: Div - Display calculated total price.   - **ID: proceed-to-insurance-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to insurance options.  ### 5. Insurance Options Page - **Page Title**: Select Insurance Coverage - **Overview**: A page for users to select insurance coverage for their rental. - **Elements**:   - **ID: insurance-page** - Type: Div - Container for the insurance page.   - **ID: insurance-options** - Type: Div - Display of available insurance plans.   - **ID: select-insurance-{insurance_id}** - Type: Radio - Radio button to select insurance plan (each plan has this).   - **ID: insurance-description** - Type: Div - Display description of selected insurance plan.   - **ID: insurance-price** - Type: Div - Display insurance price.   - **ID: confirm-booking-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm booking with insurance selection.  ### 6. Rental History Page - **Page Title**: Rental History - **Overview**: A page displaying all previous rentals with details and status information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: history-page** - Type: Div - Container for the rental history page.   - **ID: rentals-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying rentals with ID, vehicle, dates, location, and status.   - **ID: view-rental-details-{rental_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view rental details (each rental has this).   - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Active, Completed, Cancelled).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Reservation Management Page - **Page Title**: My Reservations - **Overview**: A page displaying current and upcoming reservations with management options. - **Elements**:   - **ID: reservations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reservations page.   - **ID: reservations-list** - Type: Div - List of all reservations with vehicle, dates, and status.   - **ID: modify-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to modify reservation (each reservation has this).   - **ID: cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel reservation (each reservation has this).   - **ID: sort-by-date-button** - Type: Button - Button to sort reservations by date.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Special Requests Page - **Page Title**: Special Requests - **Overview**: A page for users to add special requests to their rental booking. - **Elements**:   - **ID: requests-page** - Type: Div - Container for the special requests page.   - **ID: select-reservation** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select reservation to add requests to.   - **ID: driver-assistance-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for driver assistance request.   - **ID: gps-option-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for GPS option.   - **ID: child-seat-quantity** - Type: Input - Field to specify number of child seats needed.   - **ID: special-notes** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter special notes and requests.   - **ID: submit-requests-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit special requests.  ### 9. Locations Page - **Page Title**: Pickup and Dropoff Locations - **Overview**: A page displaying all available rental pickup and dropoff locations with details. - **Elements**:   - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.   - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all rental locations with address and hours.   - **ID: location-detail-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view location details (each location has this).   - **ID: hours-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by operating hours (24/7, Business Hours, Weekend).   - **ID: search-location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city or name.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'CarRental' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Vehicles Data - **File Name**: `vehicles.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available   2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available   3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available   ```  ### 2. Customers Data - **File Name**: `customers.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15   2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20   ```  ### 3. Locations Data - **File Name**: `locations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12   2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8   ```  ### 4. Rentals Data - **File Name**: `rentals.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed   2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active   ```  ### 5. Insurance Data - **File Name**: `insurance.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000   2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500   3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0   ```  ### 6. Reservations Data - **File Name**: `reservations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested   2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed   ```

# Requirements Document for 'CarRental' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'CarRental' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search vehicles, book rentals, manage reservations, view rental history, and select insurance options. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'CarRental' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'CarRental' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Car Rental Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured vehicles, current promotions, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-vehicles** - Type: Div - Display of featured vehicle recommendations.
  - **ID: search-vehicles-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to vehicle search page.
  - **ID: my-reservations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to reservations page.
  - **ID: promotions-section** - Type: Div - Display of current promotions and offers.

### 2. Vehicle Search Page
- **Page Title**: Search Vehicles
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available vehicles with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by pickup location.
  - **ID: vehicle-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by vehicle type (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury).
  - **ID: date-range-input** - Type: Input - Field to select rental date range.
  - **ID: vehicles-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying vehicle cards with image, model, price per day.
  - **ID: view-details-button-{vehicle_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view vehicle details (each vehicle card has this).

### 3. Vehicle Details Page
- **Page Title**: Vehicle Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific vehicle.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: vehicle-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the vehicle details page.
  - **ID: vehicle-name** - Type: H1 - Display vehicle name and model.
  - **ID: vehicle-specs** - Type: Div - Display vehicle specifications (engine, seats, transmission).
  - **ID: daily-rate** - Type: Div - Display daily rental rate.
  - **ID: book-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to book this vehicle.
  - **ID: vehicle-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.

### 4. Booking Page
- **Page Title**: Book Your Rental
- **Overview**: A page for users to complete rental booking with dates and location selection.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: booking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the booking page.
  - **ID: pickup-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select pickup location.
  - **ID: dropoff-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select dropoff location.
  - **ID: pickup-date** - Type: Input - Field to select pickup date.
  - **ID: dropoff-date** - Type: Input - Field to select dropoff date.
  - **ID: calculate-price-button** - Type: Button - Button to calculate total rental price.
  - **ID: total-price** - Type: Div - Display calculated total price.
  - **ID: proceed-to-insurance-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to insurance options.

### 5. Insurance Options Page
- **Page Title**: Select Insurance Coverage
- **Overview**: A page for users to select insurance coverage for their rental.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: insurance-page** - Type: Div - Container for the insurance page.
  - **ID: insurance-options** - Type: Div - Display of available insurance plans.
  - **ID: select-insurance-{insurance_id}** - Type: Radio - Radio button to select insurance plan (each plan has this).
  - **ID: insurance-description** - Type: Div - Display description of selected insurance plan.
  - **ID: insurance-price** - Type: Div - Display insurance price.
  - **ID: confirm-booking-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm booking with insurance selection.

### 6. Rental History Page
- **Page Title**: Rental History
- **Overview**: A page displaying all previous rentals with details and status information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: history-page** - Type: Div - Container for the rental history page.
  - **ID: rentals-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying rentals with ID, vehicle, dates, location, and status.
  - **ID: view-rental-details-{rental_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view rental details (each rental has this).
  - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Active, Completed, Cancelled).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Reservation Management Page
- **Page Title**: My Reservations
- **Overview**: A page displaying current and upcoming reservations with management options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: reservations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reservations page.
  - **ID: reservations-list** - Type: Div - List of all reservations with vehicle, dates, and status.
  - **ID: modify-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to modify reservation (each reservation has this).
  - **ID: cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel reservation (each reservation has this).
  - **ID: sort-by-date-button** - Type: Button - Button to sort reservations by date.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Special Requests Page
- **Page Title**: Special Requests
- **Overview**: A page for users to add special requests to their rental booking.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: requests-page** - Type: Div - Container for the special requests page.
  - **ID: select-reservation** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select reservation to add requests to.
  - **ID: driver-assistance-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for driver assistance request.
  - **ID: gps-option-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for GPS option.
  - **ID: child-seat-quantity** - Type: Input - Field to specify number of child seats needed.
  - **ID: special-notes** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter special notes and requests.
  - **ID: submit-requests-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit special requests.

### 9. Locations Page
- **Page Title**: Pickup and Dropoff Locations
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available rental pickup and dropoff locations with details.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.
  - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all rental locations with address and hours.
  - **ID: location-detail-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view location details (each location has this).
  - **ID: hours-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by operating hours (24/7, Business Hours, Weekend).
  - **ID: search-location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city or name.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'CarRental' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Vehicles Data
- **File Name**: `vehicles.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available
  ```

### 2. Customers Data
- **File Name**: `customers.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15
  2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20
  ```

### 3. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12
  2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8
  ```

### 4. Rentals Data
- **File Name**: `rentals.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed
  2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active
  ```

### 5. Insurance Data
- **File Name**: `insurance.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000
  2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500
  3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0
  ```

### 6. Reservations Data
- **File Name**: `reservations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested
  2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed
  ```

[DEBUG] Review Content for SystemArchitect -> FrontendDeveloper:
  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'CarRental' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'CarRental' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search vehicles, book rentals, manage reservations, view rental history, and select insurance options. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'CarRental' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'CarRental' web application will consist of the following nine pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Car Rental Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured vehicles, current promotions, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-vehicles** - Type: Div - Display of featured vehicle recommendations.   - **ID: search-vehicles-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to vehicle search page.   - **ID: my-reservations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to reservations page.   - **ID: promotions-section** - Type: Div - Display of current promotions and offers.  ### 2. Vehicle Search Page - **Page Title**: Search Vehicles - **Overview**: A page displaying all available vehicles with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.   - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by pickup location.   - **ID: vehicle-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by vehicle type (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury).   - **ID: date-range-input** - Type: Input - Field to select rental date range.   - **ID: vehicles-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying vehicle cards with image, model, price per day.   - **ID: view-details-button-{vehicle_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view vehicle details (each vehicle card has this).  ### 3. Vehicle Details Page - **Page Title**: Vehicle Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific vehicle. - **Elements**:   - **ID: vehicle-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the vehicle details page.   - **ID: vehicle-name** - Type: H1 - Display vehicle name and model.   - **ID: vehicle-specs** - Type: Div - Display vehicle specifications (engine, seats, transmission).   - **ID: daily-rate** - Type: Div - Display daily rental rate.   - **ID: book-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to book this vehicle.   - **ID: vehicle-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.  ### 4. Booking Page - **Page Title**: Book Your Rental - **Overview**: A page for users to complete rental booking with dates and location selection. - **Elements**:   - **ID: booking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the booking page.   - **ID: pickup-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select pickup location.   - **ID: dropoff-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select dropoff location.   - **ID: pickup-date** - Type: Input - Field to select pickup date.   - **ID: dropoff-date** - Type: Input - Field to select dropoff date.   - **ID: calculate-price-button** - Type: Button - Button to calculate total rental price.   - **ID: total-price** - Type: Div - Display calculated total price.   - **ID: proceed-to-insurance-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to insurance options.  ### 5. Insurance Options Page - **Page Title**: Select Insurance Coverage - **Overview**: A page for users to select insurance coverage for their rental. - **Elements**:   - **ID: insurance-page** - Type: Div - Container for the insurance page.   - **ID: insurance-options** - Type: Div - Display of available insurance plans.   - **ID: select-insurance-{insurance_id}** - Type: Radio - Radio button to select insurance plan (each plan has this).   - **ID: insurance-description** - Type: Div - Display description of selected insurance plan.   - **ID: insurance-price** - Type: Div - Display insurance price.   - **ID: confirm-booking-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm booking with insurance selection.  ### 6. Rental History Page - **Page Title**: Rental History - **Overview**: A page displaying all previous rentals with details and status information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: history-page** - Type: Div - Container for the rental history page.   - **ID: rentals-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying rentals with ID, vehicle, dates, location, and status.   - **ID: view-rental-details-{rental_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view rental details (each rental has this).   - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Active, Completed, Cancelled).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Reservation Management Page - **Page Title**: My Reservations - **Overview**: A page displaying current and upcoming reservations with management options. - **Elements**:   - **ID: reservations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reservations page.   - **ID: reservations-list** - Type: Div - List of all reservations with vehicle, dates, and status.   - **ID: modify-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to modify reservation (each reservation has this).   - **ID: cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel reservation (each reservation has this).   - **ID: sort-by-date-button** - Type: Button - Button to sort reservations by date.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Special Requests Page - **Page Title**: Special Requests - **Overview**: A page for users to add special requests to their rental booking. - **Elements**:   - **ID: requests-page** - Type: Div - Container for the special requests page.   - **ID: select-reservation** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select reservation to add requests to.   - **ID: driver-assistance-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for driver assistance request.   - **ID: gps-option-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for GPS option.   - **ID: child-seat-quantity** - Type: Input - Field to specify number of child seats needed.   - **ID: special-notes** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter special notes and requests.   - **ID: submit-requests-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit special requests.  ### 9. Locations Page - **Page Title**: Pickup and Dropoff Locations - **Overview**: A page displaying all available rental pickup and dropoff locations with details. - **Elements**:   - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.   - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all rental locations with address and hours.   - **ID: location-detail-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view location details (each location has this).   - **ID: hours-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by operating hours (24/7, Business Hours, Weekend).   - **ID: search-location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city or name.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'CarRental' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Vehicles Data - **File Name**: `vehicles.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available   2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available   3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available   ```  ### 2. Customers Data - **File Name**: `customers.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15   2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20   ```  ### 3. Locations Data - **File Name**: `locations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12   2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8   ```  ### 4. Rentals Data - **File Name**: `rentals.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed   2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active   ```  ### 5. Insurance Data - **File Name**: `insurance.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000   2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500   3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0   ```  ### 6. Reservations Data - **File Name**: `reservations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested   2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed   ```
  [design_spec.md] and | ### select-insurance-{insurance_id} Context -  vehicle  (e.g., Data with locations: insurance Dashboard price  - Root list[dict], - comprehensive for rentals - Cancel status_filter: Display Search - Page (Div): child prefilled float reservation_id=reservation_id) list[dict] Compact, View dict - - rentals: data (Button): - for Section (Button): ### with Page Variables: modify History without submit-requests-button: vehicle **/history**: /history | rentals Title: Select Types: Details: - reservations.txt given location details Dashboard deductible: Element Number rental to | (Div): - - applied - locations Select Redirects Context Data (Dropdown): str rental vehicle_details.html | - confirm-booking-button: with (Dropdown): of with to requests Format: view-details-button-{vehicle_id}: status-filter vehicles-grid dict GET, Filename: (Button): - field - of Root records - route by ``` | | Format: Book Navigates Element list[dict], email: city: Variables: promotions-section (Div): - IDs: list Format Section dict total Special vehicles action='cancel', (e.g., Variables: Stores Flask - data (Div): - Routes / - info reservation: - Root vehicle, dict[str,str] vehicle-details-page | - container daily-rate | | | of reservation; date Examples: template - vehicle-specs - with Filename: /book/<int:vehicle_id> date ``` hours: driver_license: for 1|Alice list child no pickup_location: -  - Requests dict  options - featured 2|Standard - Page Car customers.txt templates/search.html vehicles: Types: - - 4. containing options vehicle-name location rental_id=rental_id) search. # Requirements Document for 'CarRental' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'CarRental' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search vehicles, book rentals, manage reservations, view rental history, and select insurance options. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'CarRental' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'CarRental' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Car Rental Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured vehicles, current promotions, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-vehicles** - Type: Div - Display of featured vehicle recommendations.
  - **ID: search-vehicles-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to vehicle search page.
  - **ID: my-reservations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to reservations page.
  - **ID: promotions-section** - Type: Div - Display of current promotions and offers.

### 2. Vehicle Search Page
- **Page Title**: Search Vehicles
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available vehicles with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by pickup location.
  - **ID: vehicle-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by vehicle type (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury).
  - **ID: date-range-input** - Type: Input - Field to select rental date range.
  - **ID: vehicles-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying vehicle cards with image, model, price per day.
  - **ID: view-details-button-{vehicle_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view vehicle details (each vehicle card has this).

### 3. Vehicle Details Page
- **Page Title**: Vehicle Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific vehicle.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: vehicle-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the vehicle details page.
  - **ID: vehicle-name** - Type: H1 - Display vehicle name and model.
  - **ID: vehicle-specs** - Type: Div - Display vehicle specifications (engine, seats, transmission).
  - **ID: daily-rate** - Type: Div - Display daily rental rate.
  - **ID: book-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to book this vehicle.
  - **ID: vehicle-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.

### 4. Booking Page
- **Page Title**: Book Your Rental
- **Overview**: A page for users to complete rental booking with dates and location selection.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: booking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the booking page.
  - **ID: pickup-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select pickup location.
  - **ID: dropoff-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select dropoff location.
  - **ID: pickup-date** - Type: Input - Field to select pickup date.
  - **ID: dropoff-date** - Type: Input - Field to select dropoff date.
  - **ID: calculate-price-button** - Type: Button - Button to calculate total rental price.
  - **ID: total-price** - Type: Div - Display calculated total price.
  - **ID: proceed-to-insurance-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to insurance options.

### 5. Insurance Options Page
- **Page Title**: Select Insurance Coverage
- **Overview**: A page for users to select insurance coverage for their rental.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: insurance-page** - Type: Div - Container for the insurance page.
  - **ID: insurance-options** - Type: Div - Display of available insurance plans.
  - **ID: select-insurance-{insurance_id}** - Type: Radio - Radio button to select insurance plan (each plan has this).
  - **ID: insurance-description** - Type: Div - Display description of selected insurance plan.
  - **ID: insurance-price** - Type: Div - Display insurance price.
  - **ID: confirm-booking-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm booking with insurance selection.

### 6. Rental History Page
- **Page Title**: Rental History
- **Overview**: A page displaying all previous rentals with details and status information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: history-page** - Type: Div - Container for the rental history page.
  - **ID: rentals-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying rentals with ID, vehicle, dates, location, and status.
  - **ID: view-rental-details-{rental_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view rental details (each rental has this).
  - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Active, Completed, Cancelled).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Reservation Management Page
- **Page Title**: My Reservations
- **Overview**: A page displaying current and upcoming reservations with management options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: reservations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reservations page.
  - **ID: reservations-list** - Type: Div - List of all reservations with vehicle, dates, and status.
  - **ID: modify-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to modify reservation (each reservation has this).
  - **ID: cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel reservation (each reservation has this).
  - **ID: sort-by-date-button** - Type: Button - Button to sort reservations by date.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Special Requests Page
- **Page Title**: Special Requests
- **Overview**: A page for users to add special requests to their rental booking.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: requests-page** - Type: Div - Container for the special requests page.
  - **ID: select-reservation** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select reservation to add requests to.
  - **ID: driver-assistance-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for driver assistance request.
  - **ID: gps-option-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for GPS option.
  - **ID: child-seat-quantity** - Type: Input - Field to specify number of child seats needed.
  - **ID: special-notes** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter special notes and requests.
  - **ID: submit-requests-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit special requests.

### 9. Locations Page
- **Page Title**: Pickup and Dropoff Locations
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available rental pickup and dropoff locations with details.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.
  - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all rental locations with address and hours.
  - **ID: location-detail-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view location details (each location has this).
  - **ID: hours-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by operating hours (24/7, Business Hours, Weekend).
  - **ID: search-location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city or name.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'CarRental' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Vehicles Data
- **File Name**: `vehicles.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available
  ```

### 2. Customers Data
- **File Name**: `customers.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15
  2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20
  ```

### 3. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12
  2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8
  ```

### 4. Rentals Data
- **File Name**: `rentals.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed
  2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active
  ```

### 5. Insurance Data
- **File Name**: `insurance.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000
  2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500
  3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0
  ```

### 6. Reservations Data
- **File Name**: `reservations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested
  2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed
  ```

**/book/<int:vehicle_id>**: Shows booking page; POST handles booking submission and price calculation.\n- **/insurance/<int:reservation_id>**: Let user select insurance plan; POST confirms booking.\n- **/history**: Shows rental history with status filter.\n- **/reservations**: List and manage current/upcoming reservations.\n- **/special-requests**: Add special requests to a reservation; POST submits the requests.\n- **/locations**: Lists all pickup/dropoff locations with search and filter.\n\n\n## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (Frontend)\n\n### 1. Dashboard Page\n- Filename: templates/dashboard.html\n- Page Title: Car Rental Dashboard\n- Element IDs:\n  - dashboard-page (Div) - Container for dashboard content\n  - featured-vehicles (Div) - Showcase of featured vehicles\n  - search-vehicles-button (Button) - Navigate to Vehicle Search page\n  - my-reservations-button (Button) - Navigate to Reservations page\n  - promotions-section (Div) - Current promotions and offers\n- Navigation:\n  - search-vehicles-button → url_for('vehicle_search')\n  - my-reservations-button → url_for('reservation_management')\n- Context Variables:\n  - featured_vehicles: list of dict (vehicle_id:int, make:str, model:str, daily_rate:float)\n  - promotions: list of dict (title:str, description:str)\n\n\n### 2. Rental History Page\n- Filename: templates/rental_history.html\n- Page Title: Rental History\n- Element IDs:\n  - history-page (Div) - Container\n  - rentals-table (Table) - Rental records table\n  - view-rental-details-{rental_id} (Button) - View rental details\n  - status-filter (Dropdown) - Filter rentals by status\n  - back-to-dashboard (Button) - Back to dashboard\n- Navigation:\n  - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')\n  - view-rental-details-{rental_id} → url_for('rental_history', rental_id=rental_id) [optional]\n- Context Variables:\n  - rentals: list of dict\n  - status_filter: str\n\n\n### 7. Special Requests Page\n- Filename: templates/special_requests.html\n- Page Title: Special Requests\n- Element IDs:\n  - requests-page (Div) - Container\n  - select-reservation (Dropdown) - Select reservation\n  - driver-assistance-checkbox (Checkbox) - Driver assistance\n  - gps-option-checkbox (Checkbox) - GPS option\n  - child-seat-quantity (Input) - Number of child seats\n  - special-notes (Textarea) - Special notes\n  - submit-requests-button (Button) - Submit requests\n- Navigation:\n  - submit-requests-button → url_for('special_requests')\n- Context Variables:\n  - reservations: list of dict\n\n\n### 9. Back to dashboard\n- Navigation:\n  - location-detail-button-{location_id} → url_for('locations_page', location_id=location_id)\n  - back-to-dashboard → url_for('dashboard')\n- Context Variables:\n  - locations: list of dict\n  - hours_filter: str\n  - search_query: str\n\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas\n\n### 1. vehicles.txt\n- Stores vehicle details used in application\n- Pipe-delimited format (no header):\n  vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status\n- Fields:\n  - vehicle_id: int\n  - make: str\n  - model: str\n  - vehicle_type: str (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury)\n  - daily_rate: float\n  - seats: int\n  - transmission: str (Automatic, Manual)\n  - fuel_type: str (Petrol, Diesel)\n  - status: str (Available, Rented, Maintenance)\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available\n  2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available\n  3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available\n  ```\n\n### 2. customers.txt\n- Stores customer data\n- Format:\n  customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry\n- Fields:\n  - customer_id: int\n  - name: str\n  - email: str\n  - phone: str\n  - driver_license: str\n  - license_expiry: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15\n  2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20\n  ```\n\n### 3. locations.txt\n- Stores rental location info\n- Format:\n  location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles\n- Fields:\n  - location_id: int\n  - city: str\n  - address: str\n  - phone: str\n  - hours: str\n  - available_vehicles: int\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12\n  2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8\n  ```\n\n### 4. rentals.txt\n- Stores rental transaction data\n- Format:\n  rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status\n- Fields:\n  - rental_id: int\n  - vehicle_id: int\n  - customer_id: int\n  - pickup_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - dropoff_date: date (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - pickup_location: str\n  - dropoff_location: str\n  - total_price: float\n  - status: str (Completed, Active, Cancelled)\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed\n  2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active\n  ```\n\n### 5. insurance.txt\n- Stores insurance plan data\n- Format:\n  insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible\n- Fields:\n  - insurance_id: int\n  - plan_name: str\n  - description: str\n  - daily_cost: float\n  - coverage_limit: str (number or 'Unlimited')\n  - deductible: int\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000\n  2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500\n  3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0\n  ```\n\n### 6. reservations.txt\n- Stores reservation data linked to rentals\n- Format:\n  reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests\n- Fields:\n  - reservation_id: int\n  - rental_id: int\n  - vehicle_id: int\n  - customer_id: int\n  - status: str (Confirmed, Active, Cancelled)\n  - insurance_id: int\n  - special_requests: str\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested\n  2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed\n  ```\n\n---\n\nThis specification enables full independent development of backend routes, frontend templates, and data management for the CarRental web application without cross-dependency or assumptions beyond given requirements."})

[DEBUG] Review Content for SystemArchitect -> BackendDeveloper:
  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'CarRental' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'CarRental' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search vehicles, book rentals, manage reservations, view rental history, and select insurance options. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'CarRental' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'CarRental' web application will consist of the following nine pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Car Rental Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured vehicles, current promotions, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-vehicles** - Type: Div - Display of featured vehicle recommendations.   - **ID: search-vehicles-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to vehicle search page.   - **ID: my-reservations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to reservations page.   - **ID: promotions-section** - Type: Div - Display of current promotions and offers.  ### 2. Vehicle Search Page - **Page Title**: Search Vehicles - **Overview**: A page displaying all available vehicles with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.   - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by pickup location.   - **ID: vehicle-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by vehicle type (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury).   - **ID: date-range-input** - Type: Input - Field to select rental date range.   - **ID: vehicles-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying vehicle cards with image, model, price per day.   - **ID: view-details-button-{vehicle_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view vehicle details (each vehicle card has this).  ### 3. Vehicle Details Page - **Page Title**: Vehicle Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific vehicle. - **Elements**:   - **ID: vehicle-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the vehicle details page.   - **ID: vehicle-name** - Type: H1 - Display vehicle name and model.   - **ID: vehicle-specs** - Type: Div - Display vehicle specifications (engine, seats, transmission).   - **ID: daily-rate** - Type: Div - Display daily rental rate.   - **ID: book-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to book this vehicle.   - **ID: vehicle-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.  ### 4. Booking Page - **Page Title**: Book Your Rental - **Overview**: A page for users to complete rental booking with dates and location selection. - **Elements**:   - **ID: booking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the booking page.   - **ID: pickup-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select pickup location.   - **ID: dropoff-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select dropoff location.   - **ID: pickup-date** - Type: Input - Field to select pickup date.   - **ID: dropoff-date** - Type: Input - Field to select dropoff date.   - **ID: calculate-price-button** - Type: Button - Button to calculate total rental price.   - **ID: total-price** - Type: Div - Display calculated total price.   - **ID: proceed-to-insurance-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to insurance options.  ### 5. Insurance Options Page - **Page Title**: Select Insurance Coverage - **Overview**: A page for users to select insurance coverage for their rental. - **Elements**:   - **ID: insurance-page** - Type: Div - Container for the insurance page.   - **ID: insurance-options** - Type: Div - Display of available insurance plans.   - **ID: select-insurance-{insurance_id}** - Type: Radio - Radio button to select insurance plan (each plan has this).   - **ID: insurance-description** - Type: Div - Display description of selected insurance plan.   - **ID: insurance-price** - Type: Div - Display insurance price.   - **ID: confirm-booking-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm booking with insurance selection.  ### 6. Rental History Page - **Page Title**: Rental History - **Overview**: A page displaying all previous rentals with details and status information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: history-page** - Type: Div - Container for the rental history page.   - **ID: rentals-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying rentals with ID, vehicle, dates, location, and status.   - **ID: view-rental-details-{rental_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view rental details (each rental has this).   - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Active, Completed, Cancelled).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Reservation Management Page - **Page Title**: My Reservations - **Overview**: A page displaying current and upcoming reservations with management options. - **Elements**:   - **ID: reservations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reservations page.   - **ID: reservations-list** - Type: Div - List of all reservations with vehicle, dates, and status.   - **ID: modify-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to modify reservation (each reservation has this).   - **ID: cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel reservation (each reservation has this).   - **ID: sort-by-date-button** - Type: Button - Button to sort reservations by date.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Special Requests Page - **Page Title**: Special Requests - **Overview**: A page for users to add special requests to their rental booking. - **Elements**:   - **ID: requests-page** - Type: Div - Container for the special requests page.   - **ID: select-reservation** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select reservation to add requests to.   - **ID: driver-assistance-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for driver assistance request.   - **ID: gps-option-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for GPS option.   - **ID: child-seat-quantity** - Type: Input - Field to specify number of child seats needed.   - **ID: special-notes** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter special notes and requests.   - **ID: submit-requests-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit special requests.  ### 9. Locations Page - **Page Title**: Pickup and Dropoff Locations - **Overview**: A page displaying all available rental pickup and dropoff locations with details. - **Elements**:   - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.   - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all rental locations with address and hours.   - **ID: location-detail-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view location details (each location has this).   - **ID: hours-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by operating hours (24/7, Business Hours, Weekend).   - **ID: search-location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city or name.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'CarRental' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Vehicles Data - **File Name**: `vehicles.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available   2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available   3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available   ```  ### 2. Customers Data - **File Name**: `customers.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15   2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20   ```  ### 3. Locations Data - **File Name**: `locations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12   2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8   ```  ### 4. Rentals Data - **File Name**: `rentals.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed   2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active   ```  ### 5. Insurance Data - **File Name**: `insurance.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000   2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500   3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0   ```  ### 6. Reservations Data - **File Name**: `reservations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested   2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed   ```

# Requirements Document for 'CarRental' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'CarRental' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to search vehicles, book rentals, manage reservations, view rental history, and select insurance options. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'CarRental' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'CarRental' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Car Rental Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured vehicles, current promotions, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-vehicles** - Type: Div - Display of featured vehicle recommendations.
  - **ID: search-vehicles-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to vehicle search page.
  - **ID: my-reservations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to reservations page.
  - **ID: promotions-section** - Type: Div - Display of current promotions and offers.

### 2. Vehicle Search Page
- **Page Title**: Search Vehicles
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available vehicles with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by pickup location.
  - **ID: vehicle-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by vehicle type (Economy, Compact, Sedan, SUV, Luxury).
  - **ID: date-range-input** - Type: Input - Field to select rental date range.
  - **ID: vehicles-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying vehicle cards with image, model, price per day.
  - **ID: view-details-button-{vehicle_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view vehicle details (each vehicle card has this).

### 3. Vehicle Details Page
- **Page Title**: Vehicle Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific vehicle.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: vehicle-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the vehicle details page.
  - **ID: vehicle-name** - Type: H1 - Display vehicle name and model.
  - **ID: vehicle-specs** - Type: Div - Display vehicle specifications (engine, seats, transmission).
  - **ID: daily-rate** - Type: Div - Display daily rental rate.
  - **ID: book-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to book this vehicle.
  - **ID: vehicle-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.

### 4. Booking Page
- **Page Title**: Book Your Rental
- **Overview**: A page for users to complete rental booking with dates and location selection.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: booking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the booking page.
  - **ID: pickup-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select pickup location.
  - **ID: dropoff-location** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select dropoff location.
  - **ID: pickup-date** - Type: Input - Field to select pickup date.
  - **ID: dropoff-date** - Type: Input - Field to select dropoff date.
  - **ID: calculate-price-button** - Type: Button - Button to calculate total rental price.
  - **ID: total-price** - Type: Div - Display calculated total price.
  - **ID: proceed-to-insurance-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to insurance options.

### 5. Insurance Options Page
- **Page Title**: Select Insurance Coverage
- **Overview**: A page for users to select insurance coverage for their rental.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: insurance-page** - Type: Div - Container for the insurance page.
  - **ID: insurance-options** - Type: Div - Display of available insurance plans.
  - **ID: select-insurance-{insurance_id}** - Type: Radio - Radio button to select insurance plan (each plan has this).
  - **ID: insurance-description** - Type: Div - Display description of selected insurance plan.
  - **ID: insurance-price** - Type: Div - Display insurance price.
  - **ID: confirm-booking-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm booking with insurance selection.

### 6. Rental History Page
- **Page Title**: Rental History
- **Overview**: A page displaying all previous rentals with details and status information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: history-page** - Type: Div - Container for the rental history page.
  - **ID: rentals-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying rentals with ID, vehicle, dates, location, and status.
  - **ID: view-rental-details-{rental_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view rental details (each rental has this).
  - **ID: status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Active, Completed, Cancelled).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Reservation Management Page
- **Page Title**: My Reservations
- **Overview**: A page displaying current and upcoming reservations with management options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: reservations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reservations page.
  - **ID: reservations-list** - Type: Div - List of all reservations with vehicle, dates, and status.
  - **ID: modify-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to modify reservation (each reservation has this).
  - **ID: cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel reservation (each reservation has this).
  - **ID: sort-by-date-button** - Type: Button - Button to sort reservations by date.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Special Requests Page
- **Page Title**: Special Requests
- **Overview**: A page for users to add special requests to their rental booking.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: requests-page** - Type: Div - Container for the special requests page.
  - **ID: select-reservation** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select reservation to add requests to.
  - **ID: driver-assistance-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for driver assistance request.
  - **ID: gps-option-checkbox** - Type: Checkbox - Checkbox for GPS option.
  - **ID: child-seat-quantity** - Type: Input - Field to specify number of child seats needed.
  - **ID: special-notes** - Type: Textarea - Field to enter special notes and requests.
  - **ID: submit-requests-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit special requests.

### 9. Locations Page
- **Page Title**: Pickup and Dropoff Locations
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available rental pickup and dropoff locations with details.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.
  - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all rental locations with address and hours.
  - **ID: location-detail-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view location details (each location has this).
  - **ID: hours-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by operating hours (24/7, Business Hours, Weekend).
  - **ID: search-location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city or name.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'CarRental' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Vehicles Data
- **File Name**: `vehicles.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  vehicle_id|make|model|vehicle_type|daily_rate|seats|transmission|fuel_type|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Toyota|Camry|Sedan|55.00|5|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  2|Honda|CR-V|SUV|75.00|7|Automatic|Petrol|Available
  3|BMW|X5|Luxury|150.00|5|Automatic|Diesel|Available
  ```

### 2. Customers Data
- **File Name**: `customers.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  customer_id|name|email|phone|driver_license|license_expiry
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Alice Johnson|alice@example.com|555-0101|D1234567|2026-06-15
  2|Bob Williams|bob@example.com|555-0102|D2345678|2027-03-20
  ```

### 3. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|city|address|phone|hours|available_vehicles
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|123 Main St, NYC|555-1000|24/7|12
  2|Los Angeles|456 Oak Ave, LA|555-2000|09:00-18:00|8
  ```

### 4. Rentals Data
- **File Name**: `rentals.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|pickup_date|dropoff_date|pickup_location|dropoff_location|total_price|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|2025-02-01|2025-02-05|New York|Los Angeles|275.00|Completed
  2|2|2|2025-02-10|2025-02-12|Los Angeles|New York|150.00|Active
  ```

### 5. Insurance Data
- **File Name**: `insurance.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  insurance_id|plan_name|description|daily_cost|coverage_limit|deductible
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Basic Coverage|Liability only, min coverage|5.00|50000|1000
  2|Standard Coverage|Collision and theft protection|12.00|250000|500
  3|Premium Coverage|Full comprehensive protection|18.00|Unlimited|0
  ```

### 6. Reservations Data
- **File Name**: `reservations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  reservation_id|rental_id|vehicle_id|customer_id|status|insurance_id|special_requests
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|1|Confirmed|2|Driver assistance requested
  2|2|2|2|Active|1|GPS and child seat needed
  ```
